# Surrenderless — project state (source of truth)

This document aligns Cursor, ChatGPT, and humans on **product intent**, **current reality**, and **where to invest**. It describes the repo as of its last update; verify against code when in doubt.

---

## 1. True product goal

**Surrenderless is a chat-first action assistant.** The user should eventually **only chat** with Surrenderless — not manually hop across forms, tabs, and external sites as the primary experience. The user **chats**; the app:

- Gathers facts **conversationally**
- **Structures** the case
- **Collects and organizes** proof (screenshots, receipts, emails, and similar — tied to the case in-app)
- **Prepares** submissions, messages, and complaints for review (in-app previews and drafts today; more automation later where feasible)
- Gets **approval**
- **Submits or queues** actions when technically (and legally) possible
- **Tracks** confirmations, filings, and follow-ups
- **Carries** the issue from beginning to end

Existing **`/justice/*`** pages (intake form, evidence page, prep surfaces, etc.) are **interim scaffolding** toward that single conversational shell — not the final product shape.

Anything that permanently treats “open another tab and paste into a government form” as the final experience is **out of scope for the long-term product**, even if it is useful as an interim step.

---

## 2. Current reality

The shipped experience is **still a multi-page Consumer Justice case-management scaffold** (many prep surfaces and manual filing paths), but **navigation across hub, preview, plan, and prep surfaces now promotes AI conversational chat intake first** toward the long-term **chat-first action** goal (§1): describe the issue once in chat, structure the case, review a submission preview, approve, then follow evidence, filings, tasks, and plan guidance inside the app (filing/queueing only where feasible today; much remains manual prep and external filing).


- **Stack:** Next.js (App Router), TypeScript, **Clerk** (auth), **Supabase** (persistence via service-role API routes), **REST API routes**, **session/local storage** for active case + timeline mirror.
- **UX:** Multi-page **justice** routes (`/justice/*`): **`/justice`** workspace hub (thin landing); **primary chat intake** — **AI conversational** intake at **`/justice/chat-ai`** (§2; hub/header **Chat intake** → **`/justice/chat-ai`**; preview empty-state/footer **Chat intake** → **`/justice/chat-ai`**; §2 **Justice-wide navigation alignment**); **step-by-step scripted** intake at **`/justice/chat`** (labeled **Step-by-step chat** where linked; **unchanged** scripted Q&A); **structured form** intake at **`/justice/intake`** (labeled **Structured form** / **Edit structured form** where linked; loads saved answers for direct field edit); action plan; **`/justice/preview`** (in-app **submission draft preview**: deterministic text from **`buildSubmissionDraftPreview.ts`** remains **source of truth / fallback**; optional **AI-assisted** draft via signed-in **`POST /api/justice/preview-draft`** (Clerk **`getUserOr401`**, **`rateLimit`**, server-only **`OPENAI_API_KEY`**, prompts from **`buildSubmissionDraftAiPrompt.ts`**); UI copy states case details are sent to **OpenAI**; AI output is **review-only**, nothing filed; **no** DB writes, schema migrations, embedded browser, or filing automation for AI; destination selector from current justice destinations; **“I reviewed this draft”** before **Continue to action plan** → **`/justice/plan`**), per-destination prep pages, dedicated evidence page, saved cases, **`/justice/handling`** **Handling workbench** (§2 **Handling workbench — internal triage surface**), archived cases, packet (aggregate/export). **`/justice/plan`** links to **`/justice/preview`** from the **case packet** area. **`/justice/intake`**, **`/justice/chat`**, and **`/justice/chat-ai`** share **`src/lib/justice/commitIntakeToSessionAndServer.ts`** and **`src/lib/justice/normalizeCompanyWebsite.ts`** on form + scripted chat (optional company website: bare domains like `amazon.com` → `https://amazon.com`, sentinels like `none` / `n/a` → empty string). **Create commit (default):** **`/justice/intake`**, **`/justice/chat`**, and **new** **`/justice/chat-ai`** sessions — new case id, **`case_started`**, optional **`POST /api/justice/cases`**, **`intake_completed`**, then **`router.push("/justice/preview")`** (**`/justice/plan`** after preview continue). **Update commit:** **`/justice/chat-ai`** when an active case was hydrated (§2) — preserve case id/timeline, **`PATCH`** when signed in + UUID, no **`POST`**. **`/justice/chat`** and **`/justice/chat-ai`** use **`src/lib/justice/buildJusticeIntake.ts`** (**`buildJusticeIntakeFromParts`**, **`justiceIntakeToBuildJusticeIntakeParts`**, **`validateContactProofForIntake`**; §2). **`POST /api/justice/intake-chat`** powers AI turns on **`/justice/chat-ai`** (contract unchanged; §2).
- **Justice workspace hub (`/justice`):** **`/justice`** is shipped as a **thin**, **intentionally lightweight** Consumer Justice **workspace** landing — **not** a dashboard rewrite and **not** a replacement for **`/justice/plan`**. Copy explains that Surrenderless **organizes consumer issues into an action plan**, prepares **drafts, checklists, and records** for the user to use, and **does not file or submit complaints automatically**. Hub copy **recommends chat intake** and notes that **form intake** remains available for users who prefer the full structured form. **`src/app/justice/JusticeHubWorkspaceBody.tsx`** (single client mount **read-only**) renders the hub link list and, when **`readValidLocalJusticeIntake()`** finds valid **`sessionStorage`** intake, a compact **Current case** card — company name, category/product labels, submission-draft status from **`readTimeline`** using **`STORAGE_CASE_ID`**, and one primary link on the **Current case** card: **`/justice/chat-ai`**, **Continue in chat** — regardless of draft-review or prepared-packet state (§2 **Justice hub — Current case primary CTA routing (`/justice`)**); checklist deep links **Review submission draft** → **`/justice/preview`** and **Review prepared case packet** → **`/justice/packet`** unchanged. The static **Continue current action plan** hub card is **omitted** when a **Current case** snapshot exists so the dynamic card is the only “next step” CTA. **Current case** display **re-refreshes client-side** when the **tab becomes visible** (`document.visibilityState === "visible"` on **`visibilitychange`**), when the **browser window regains focus** (`window` **`focus`**), and on **`storage`** (e.g. cross-tab updates to **`sessionStorage`** / shared storage) so the card is **less likely to stay stale** after **chat**, **preview**, **plan**, or other flows that mutate local intake/timeline — still using only **existing** local helpers (**`readValidLocalJusticeIntake`**, **`readTimeline`**, **`STORAGE_CASE_ID`**); **no** hub case-list **`GET`**, **no** new routes, APIs, **`rules.ts`**, commit/preview/plan semantics, schemas, timeline event **definitions**, **`commitIntakeToSessionAndServer`**, or **`/justice/preview`** / **`/justice/plan`** behavior changes beyond their existing writes to **`sessionStorage`**. **Needs more info** chat routing on **Current case** — §2 **Justice hub — Needs more info chat routing CTA on Current case (`/justice`)**; compact **Current case** readiness checklist — §2 **Justice hub — Current case compact readiness checklist (`/justice`)**; approved next-step label + status on **Current case** — §2 **Justice hub — approved next-step label and status on Current case (`/justice`)**. With **no** local intake, link cards are **Start with chat intake** (**`/justice/chat-ai`**), **Use step-by-step chat** (**`/justice/chat`**; §2), **Continue current action plan**, **Start with form intake**, **Saved cases**. **No** case-list **`GET`**, **no** session mutation from the hub (reads only; active-case evidence **`GET`** for chat routing — §2 **Justice hub — Needs more info chat routing CTA on Current case (`/justice`)**). **`src/app/components/Header.tsx`** global nav order is **Justice** → **Chat intake** (**`/justice/chat-ai`**) → **Consumer case** (form intake → **`/justice/intake`**). **No** case **`GET`** on the hub, **no** duplication of **`rules.ts`** / plan readiness / destination logic, **no** new APIs, **no** auth changes, **no** schema or new DB tables, **no** automation, **no** filing or government submission from this surface. **Hub/header ordering** for chat-first entry is **UI-only** on this surface (see next bullet). **Preview-first intake finish** (**`/justice/intake`**, **`/justice/chat`**, and **`/justice/chat-ai`** → **`/justice/preview`**) is documented in §5; hub remains **read-only** (no commit from hub). **`commitIntakeToSessionAndServer`** **create** vs **update** modes: §2 **Chat AI intake — hydrate & update commit**.
- **Justice hub — handling requested on Current case (`/justice`):** **`src/app/justice/JusticeHubWorkspaceBody.tsx`** + **`src/lib/justice/approvedNextActionHandlingDisplay.tsx`** — **read-only legacy display** when **`!(snapshot.packetApproved && snapshot.approvedNextAction)`** but session has **`handling_requested_at`** (with §2 **Justice hub — approved next-step label and status on Current case (`/justice`)**). When valid local intake exists and **`justice_approved_next_action_v1`** has **`handling_requested_at`** for **`STORAGE_CASE_ID`** (via **`readSessionApprovedNextAction`** — §2 **Approved next action shared state helpers**), the **Current case** card (inside the primary **`Link`**) shows **Surrenderless handling requested** with recorded time; optional note (**`ApprovedNextActionHandlingRequestNoteReadOnly`**); optional **Acknowledged {time}** (**`ApprovedNextActionHandlingAcknowledgedReadOnly`**); **in-app tracking only** disclaimer. Below the card (legacy path only): **display-only** queue status (§2 **Justice hub — display-only derived handling queue status**) and **View in handling workbench** (§2 **Handling workbench — active-case back-link from hub**). When **`snapshot.packetApproved && snapshot.approvedNextAction`**, interactive request/note/ack — §2 **Justice hub — Surrenderless handling request and acknowledge on Current case (`/justice`)** — replaces in-card and below-card legacy handling UI for the approved case. **In-app tracking only** — Surrenderless has **not** filed, submitted, sent, **queued externally**, or contacted anyone. **No** routing changes. Refreshes on **focus**, **`storage`**, and **visibility**. **No** schema, migration, new API route, queue worker, filing record, timeline **type**, or automation.
- **Justice hub — display-only derived handling queue status (`/justice`):** **`src/app/justice/JusticeHubWorkspaceBody.tsx`** + **`src/lib/justice/approvedNextActionHandlingDisplay.tsx`** (**`ApprovedNextActionHandlingQueueStatusReadOnly`**, **`deriveHandlingQueueDisplayStatus`**) — **visibility-only** slice completing **queue-status parity** across every surface that shows handling (with §2 **Saved cases — handling requested visibility on All cases cards**, **Handling workbench — internal triage surface**, **Packet — display-only derived handling queue status**, **Chat AI intake — display-only derived handling queue status**, and **Plan — display-only derived handling queue status**). When the **Current case** snapshot has **`handlingRequestedAt`** / **`handling_requested_at`** (session **`justice_approved_next_action_v1`** via **`readSessionApprovedNextAction`**), renders **display-only derived queue status** from existing **`handling_requested_at`** and **`handling_acknowledged_at`** / **`handlingAcknowledgedAt`** only (**no** new persisted field, **no** writes): **Queue status: Awaiting internal triage.** when **`handling_acknowledged_at`** is absent; **Queue status: Acknowledged for internal tracking triage only** when **`handling_acknowledged_at`** is set. Placed below the **Current case** card (after in-card handling disclaimer content) and before **View in handling workbench** (§2 **Handling workbench — active-case back-link from hub**). When **`handling_requested_at`** is absent, **no** queue status line. **Does not** change **`STORAGE_CASE_ID`**, request/ack/note behavior, server **`GET`**, plan/preview CTA, chat-intake hub cards, hub refresh, or workbench link. **In-app tracking only** — Surrenderless has **not** filed, submitted, sent, **queued externally**, or contacted anyone. **No** schema, migration, new API route, queue worker, **`justice_case_filings`** row, timeline **type**, browser automation, filing automation, external submission/contact/queue automation, or **`/api/submit-form`**; **nothing** filed, submitted, sent, queued externally, or contacted automatically.
- **Justice hub — handled/open handling triage note on Current case (`/justice`):** **`src/app/justice/JusticeHubWorkspaceBody.tsx`** + **`src/lib/justice/approvedNextActionHandlingDisplay.tsx`** — **copy-only** slice (with §2 **Justice hub — handling requested on Current case**, **Justice hub — display-only derived handling queue status**, **Justice hub — Surrenderless handling request and acknowledge on Current case (`/justice`)**, **Approved next action — centralized handled/open handling triage note copy**, **Saved cases — handled/open handling triage note on All cases cards**). When **`snapshot.packetApproved && snapshot.approvedNextAction`** and hydrated **`approved_next_action`** has **`handling_requested_at`**, no **`handling_acknowledged_at`**, and **`status === "completed"`**, renders **`ApprovedNextActionHandlingHandledOpenTriageNote`** with variant **`inlineAck`** below queue status and above **View in handling workbench** (§2 **Justice hub — Surrenderless handling request and acknowledge on Current case (`/justice`)**). **Legacy** path when **`!(packetApproved && approvedNextAction)`** but session snapshot has **`handling_requested_at`** + completed + unacknowledged: variant **`redirect`** via **`showHandledOpenHandlingTriageNote`** — **no** **Mark acknowledged** on that legacy path. **Hidden** when **`status !== "completed"`**, when **`handling_acknowledged_at`** is set, or when **`handling_requested_at`** is absent. **Does not** change interactive request/note/ack writes (§2 **Justice hub — Surrenderless handling request and acknowledge on Current case (`/justice`)**), queue status, workbench link, focus/**`visibilitychange`**/**`storage`** refresh, or external-action behavior. **No** schema, migration, new API route, queue worker, **`justice_case_filings`**, timeline **type**, or external submission/contact/queue automation.
- **Justice hub — handling tracking status on Current case (`/justice`):** **`src/app/justice/JusticeHubWorkspaceBody.tsx`** only — **read-only sync** slice (with §2 **Justice hub — display-only derived handling queue status (`/justice`)**, §2 **Justice hub — Surrenderless handling request and acknowledge on Current case (`/justice`)**, §2 **Handling workbench — manual action progress on handling-request triage cards (`/justice/handling`)**, §2 **Handling workbench — tracking complete queue on handling-request triage cards (`/justice/handling`)**, §2 **Saved cases — handling tracking status on All cases cards (`/justice/cases`)**, §2 **Plan — handling tracking status on prepared-packet handling callouts (`/justice/plan`)**, §2 **Chat AI intake — handling tracking status in Current action tracking (`/justice/chat-ai`)**, §2 **Packet — handling tracking status in prepared-action handling UI (`/justice/packet`)**). In **both** **Current case** handling blocks when **`handling_requested_at`** is set — **prepared-packet** path (**`snapshot.packetApproved && snapshot.approvedNextAction`**) and **legacy/session** path (**`snapshot.handlingRequestedAt`** with hydrated **`snapshot.approvedNextAction`**) — **`HubHandlingTrackingStatusReadOnly`** shows read-only **Handling tracking:** after **`ApprovedNextActionHandlingQueueStatusReadOnly`** — **Loading handling tracking context...** while **`hubReadinessLoading`**; when ready, **Handling tracking: {derived next step}** from page-local **`deriveHubManualActionNextStep`** / **`deriveHubHandlingTrackingLine`** mirroring workbench **`deriveManualActionNextStep`** gate order (basics + draft reviewed + prepared packet approved, **`approved_next_action`** status/outcome/ack/follow-up, **`evidenceCount`**, **`hasFilingRecord`** / **`hasConfirmationOnFile`** from **`filings`** parsed in extended **`refreshHubState`** — parallel **`GET /api/justice/evidence?case_id={id}`** + existing-contract **`GET /api/justice/filings?case_id={id}`** — same meaning as workbench **`handlingCaseHasFilingRecord`** / **`handlingCaseHasConfirmationOnFile`**); when gates are satisfied, **Handling tracking: Tracking complete for now.** — parity with workbench **Tracking complete** queue — §2 **Handling workbench — tracking complete queue on handling-request triage cards (`/justice/handling`)**. Nearby subcopy: **In-app tracking only — not filed or submitted.** Placed before handled/open triage note (§2 **Justice hub — handled/open handling triage note on Current case (`/justice`)**) / **View in handling workbench**. **No** new API route, **`client_state`** fields, timeline writes, workers, or queues. **Does not** change request/note/ack writes, **Needs attention** membership, plan, packet, chat-ai, cases, handling workbench, or filing/submission/contact automation. **Read-only in-app sync only** — Surrenderless has **not** filed, submitted, sent, **queued externally**, contacted anyone, or closed the real-world case. **No** schema, migration, new API route, queue worker, timeline **type**, browser automation, filing automation, external submission/contact/queue automation, or **`/api/submit-form`**.
- **Justice hub — Surrenderless handling request and acknowledge on Current case (`/justice`):** **`src/app/justice/JusticeHubWorkspaceBody.tsx`** only — **behavior** slice (with §2 **Justice hub — handling requested on Current case (`/justice`)**, §2 **Justice hub — display-only derived handling queue status (`/justice`)**, §2 **Justice hub — handled/open handling triage note on Current case (`/justice`)**, §2 **Handling workbench — active-case back-link from hub**, §2 **Plan — Surrenderless handling requested (`/justice/plan`)**, §2 **Packet — Surrenderless handling request and acknowledge on approved case packet surface (`/justice/packet`)**, §2 **Chat AI intake — handling requested in Current action tracking (`/justice/chat-ai`)**, §2 **Saved cases — acknowledge handling request from Needs attention (`/justice/cases`)**, §2 **Approved next action shared state helpers (`approvedNextActionState.ts`)**). Makes **`/justice`** a **handling entry point** on the **Current case** approved-action area (outside the primary card **`Link`**) when **`snapshot.packetApproved`** and hydrated **`snapshot.approvedNextAction`** exist — closes hub-side **internal manual-handling handoff** without leaving the workspace landing. Page-local **`handleRequestSurrenderlessHandling`**, **`handleUpdateHandlingRequestNote`**, **`handleAcknowledgeHandlingRequest`** mirror plan/packet/chat: set **`handling_requested_at`** (ISO) + optional **`handling_request_note`**; note edit via **`applyHandlingRequestNoteToApprovedNextAction`** / **`omitClearedHandlingRequestNoteFromApprovedNextAction`**; acknowledge via **`acknowledgeHandlingRequestInApprovedNextAction`** — all persist through existing signed-in **UUID** **`GET /api/justice/cases/[id]`** + **`mergeClientStateWithApprovedNextAction`** / **`mergeClientStateWithAcknowledgedHandling`** + **`PATCH`** **`client_state`** (**`mergeApprovedNextActionTrackingFields`**, **`writeSessionApprovedNextAction`**, **`refreshHubState`** display sync) preserving **`status`**, **`started_at`**, **`completed_at`**, **`outcome_note`**, **`follow_up_*`**, **`label`**, **`href`**, **`approved_at`**, and other **`approved_next_action`** fields. Writes gated on current session case (**`STORAGE_CASE_ID === snapshot.caseId`**), **`packetApproved`**, and hydrated **`approvedNextAction`**. UI via shared **`ApprovedNextActionHandlingRequestBlock`**: when **`status !== "completed"`** and **no** **`handling_requested_at`** — **Request Surrenderless handling** + optional note; when **`handling_requested_at`** and **`status !== "completed"`** — same block with **`allowEditNote`**; when **`status === "completed"`** and **`handling_requested_at`** — **`ApprovedNextActionHandlingRequestedReadOnly`**, **`ApprovedNextActionHandlingQueueStatusReadOnly`**, **`ApprovedNextActionHandlingHandledOpenTriageNote`** (**`inlineAck`**) when unacknowledged, **View in handling workbench**, and **Mark acknowledged** + **`APPROVED_NEXT_ACTION_HANDLING_ACKNOWLEDGE_HELPER`** when **`handling_acknowledged_at`** absent. In-card handling lines hidden when interactive block is shown. **Legacy** read-only session display when **`!(packetApproved && approvedNextAction)`** but **`handling_requested_at`** exists — §2 **Justice hub — handling requested on Current case (`/justice`)**; approved-packet without handling request copy now says request from **action plan, case packet, or here on the hub**. **Does not** auto-request handling on packet approval; **does not** change plan, chat-ai, cases, packet inner card, handling workbench, membership predicates, routing, APIs, schema, timeline writes, workers, queues, filing, submission, or automation. **Internal triage tracking only** — Surrenderless has **not** filed, submitted, sent, **queued externally**, or contacted anyone.
- **Justice hub — Needs more info chat routing CTA on Current case (`/justice`):** **`src/app/justice/JusticeHubWorkspaceBody.tsx`** only — **UI/navigation** slice (with §2 **Justice hub — Current case compact readiness checklist (`/justice`)**, §2 **Saved cases — Needs more info chat routing CTA (`/justice/cases`)**, §2 **Chat AI intake — hydrate & update commit**). When valid local intake exists (**Current case** card), uses **`isBasicCaseInfoReadyForEscalation`** from **`caseReadiness.ts`** on session intake (**no** predicate changes). When signed in and **`STORAGE_CASE_ID`** is a **UUID**, **`GET /api/justice/evidence?case_id={id}`** (same contract as saved cases/plan — **no** new API) on mount/focus/**`visibilitychange`**/**`storage`** refresh alongside the existing snapshot refresh; array length → saved proof/evidence count. Directly **below** the primary **Current case** **Continue in chat** link (outside the nested card link), one outline secondary **`Link`**: when **`!isBasicCaseInfoReadyForEscalation(intake)`** — **Update in chat** → **`/justice/chat-ai`**; when basics are complete, evidence count is loaded, and **`< 1`** — **Add proof in chat** → **`/justice/chat-ai`**; when ready (**basics** + at least one saved item) — **no** extra CTA. Active session case only — **no** **`activateCaseInSession`**. Primary **Current case** nested card target — §2 **Justice hub — Current case primary CTA routing (`/justice`)** (checklist inline links **unchanged**). Handling blocks below the card, hub link list, saved cases, plan, chat-ai, APIs, schema, and shared readiness logic **unchanged**. **Does not** claim filing, submission, contact, queueing, upload, storage, or automatic action by Surrenderless. **No** migration, worker, **`justice_case_filings`**, or external submission/contact/queue automation.
- **Justice hub — Current case compact readiness checklist (`/justice`):** **`src/app/justice/JusticeHubWorkspaceBody.tsx`** only — **UI/navigation** slice (with §2 **Justice hub — Needs more info chat routing CTA on Current case (`/justice`)**, §2 **Justice hub — Current case primary CTA routing (`/justice`)**, §2 **Justice hub — Current case prepared packet reviewed checklist row (`/justice`)**, §2 **Saved cases — compact readiness checklist on All cases cards (`/justice/cases`)**, §2 **Saved cases — All cases prepared packet reviewed checklist row (`/justice/cases`)**, §2 **Saved cases — Open case chat-first routing (`/justice/cases`)**, §2 **Chat AI intake — active case compact readiness checklist (Update in chat) (`/justice/chat-ai`)**, §2 **Chat AI intake — active case prepared packet reviewed checklist row (Update in chat) (`/justice/chat-ai`)**, §2 **Plan — Case readiness checklist proof CTA (`/justice/plan`)**, §2 **Plan — Case readiness checklist basics CTA (`/justice/plan`)**, §2 **Plan — Case readiness checklist draft-review CTA (`/justice/plan`)**, §2 **Plan — Case readiness checklist prepared packet reviewed row (`/justice/plan`)**, §2 **Plan — Case readiness approved-next visibility (`/justice/plan`)**, §2 **Packet — prepared packet approval checkpoint (`/justice/packet`)**). When **Current case** exists, adds compact **`<ul>`** under the primary card link and **before** existing secondary **Update in chat** / **Add proof in chat** buttons — mirrors plan **Case readiness** clarity on the hub entry surface. Uses **existing** state only (**no** new API, **no** schema): **`basicsReady`** from **`isBasicCaseInfoReadyForEscalation`** on session intake; **`evidenceCount`** after **`!evidenceLoading`** (same evidence **`GET`** as §2 **Justice hub — Needs more info chat routing CTA on Current case (`/justice`)**); **`snapshot.reviewed`** from session **`readTimeline`** / **`submission_draft_reviewed`**. Three rows: **Basic case info: yes/not yet** — when **`snapshot && !basicsReady`**, inline **Update in chat** → **`/justice/chat-ai`**; **Evidence: yes/not yet** (or **Evidence: loading...** while **`evidenceLoading`**) — when loaded and **`(evidenceCount ?? 0) < 1`**, inline **Add proof in chat** → **`/justice/chat-ai`**; **Submission draft reviewed: yes/not yet** — when **`snapshot && !snapshot.reviewed`**, inline **Review submission draft** → **`/justice/preview`**; fourth row when draft reviewed — §2 **Justice hub — Current case prepared packet reviewed checklist row (`/justice`)**. Same inline link classes as plan checklist CTAs (**`hubChecklistLinkCls`**). **Does not** change **`showUpdateInChat`**, **`showAddProofInChat`**, primary **Current case** card **`href`** / label (§2 **Justice hub — Current case primary CTA routing (`/justice`)**), evidence fetch, handling blocks, or hub link list. **Does not** claim filing, submission, contact, queueing, upload, storage, or automatic action by Surrenderless. **No** API, schema, helper, plan, preview, chat-ai, or cases changes on this slice. **No** migration, worker, **`justice_case_filings`**, or external submission/contact/queue automation.
- **Justice hub — Current case prepared packet reviewed checklist row (`/justice`):** **`src/app/justice/JusticeHubWorkspaceBody.tsx`** only — **UI/navigation** slice (with §2 **Justice hub — Current case compact readiness checklist (`/justice`)**, §2 **Justice hub — Current case primary CTA routing (`/justice`)**, §2 **Chat AI intake — active case prepared packet reviewed checklist row (Update in chat) (`/justice/chat-ai`)**, §2 **Saved cases — All cases prepared packet reviewed checklist row (`/justice/cases`)**, §2 **Plan — Case readiness checklist prepared packet reviewed row (`/justice/plan`)**, §2 **Packet — prepared packet approval checkpoint (`/justice/packet`)**, §2 **Plan — prepared packet approval surfaced (`/justice/plan`)**). Adds page-local **`STORAGE_PREPARED_PACKET_APPROVED_V1`** and **`readSessionPreparedPacketApproved(caseId)`** (same JSON map pattern as preview/plan/chat-ai). Extends **`readSnapshotFromLocalSession`** / **`CurrentCaseSnapshot`** with **`packetApproved: readSessionPreparedPacketApproved(caseId)`** when **`caseId`** exists — refreshed on existing **`refreshHubState`** (focus/**`storage`**/**`visibilitychange`** — **no** new listeners). In **Current case** compact checklist **`<ul>`**, **after** **Submission draft reviewed**, **only when** **`snapshot.reviewed`**: **Prepared case packet reviewed: yes** when **`packetApproved`**; **Prepared case packet reviewed: not yet** with inline **Review prepared case packet** → **`/justice/packet`** when not approved (**`hubChecklistLinkCls`**). **Navigation/readiness only** — closes hub recovery gap between draft review and packet approval (parity with chat-ai). **Does not** change evidence **`GET`**, handling blocks, approved-next labels, **Update in chat** / **Add proof in chat**, primary card **`href`** / **`primaryLabel`** (§2 **Justice hub — Current case primary CTA routing (`/justice`)**), routes, APIs, schema, handlers, or shared libs. **Session-only** for packet approval on hub (**no** case **`GET`** on this slice). **In-app tracking only** — Surrenderless has **not** filed, submitted, sent, or contacted anyone. **No** schema, migration, new API route, queue worker, browser automation, filing automation, or timeline **type**; **nothing** filed, submitted, sent, queued externally, uploaded, stored, or contacted automatically.
- **Justice hub — Current case primary CTA routing (`/justice`):** **`src/app/justice/JusticeHubWorkspaceBody.tsx`** only — **UI/navigation** slice (with §2 **Justice hub — Current case compact readiness checklist (`/justice`)**, §2 **Justice hub — Current case prepared packet reviewed checklist row (`/justice`)**, §2 **Saved cases — Open case chat-first routing (`/justice/cases`)**, §2 **Chat AI intake — hydrate & update commit**). - **Justice workspace recovery routing (`/justice` fallback):** When a Consumer Justice page **cannot hydrate or resume a usable active case** (e.g. no valid local intake and **no server row** after **`GET /api/justice/cases`**, plan **GET**/list **hydrate** failures / empty list, **`useJusticeActionPageHydration`** unable to hydrate, or analogous **missing `STORAGE_CASE_ID` / intake** escapes on routed surfaces aligned with this pattern), **`router.replace("/justice")`** or **`router.push("/justice")`** (**and matching `Link` destinations** where the same UX intent applies) lands the user on the **`/justice`** workspace hub — the **recovery hub** for missing / **no-case** / **failed-resume** states (replacing earlier **`/justice/intake`**-only redirects for those outcomes). **`/justice`** preserves **chat-first recovery** (**Start with chat intake** is first on the hub) while **`Start with form intake`** stays one click away. **Routing / copy-only** slice: **no** changes to **`rules.ts`**, recommendation logic, destination ordering, schemas, **API** route implementations (handlers, payloads, responses), auth guards, **`commitIntakeToSessionAndServer`** or other **persistence**/session commit behavior, timeline event **semantics**, **`/justice/preview`** deterministic or AI-assisted draft **generation**, filing automation, or filing/submission flows.

- **Chat intake — shared `JusticeIntake` builder (scripted `/justice/chat` + AI `/justice/chat-ai` + structured alignment):** **`src/lib/justice/buildJusticeIntake.ts`** centralizes **`BuildJusticeIntakeParts`** defaults and conversion: **`defaultBuildJusticeIntakeParts()`**, forward **`buildJusticeIntakeFromParts`** (trim strings, **`normalizeCompanyWebsite`** on scripted/AI paths that use it, merge **`money_amount`** + **`desired_resolution`** into **`money_involved`** with separator **` — Desired outcome: `**, contact fields only when **`already_contacted === "yes"`**, optional **`consumer_us_state`**), and reverse **`justiceIntakeToBuildJusticeIntakeParts`** (hydrate saved **`JusticeIntake`** from **`sessionStorage`** — conservative split of **`money_involved`** on that separator or hyphen variant, safe contact enums, **`already_contacted`** only **`yes`** when stored as yes). **Scripted** **`/justice/chat`** and **AI** **`/justice/chat-ai`** both produce the **same `JusticeIntake`** shape before commit. **`parseIntakeChatAiResponse.ts`** imports shared **`defaultBuildJusticeIntakeParts`** (re-exported) instead of duplicating defaults. **Post-intake rail:** build intake → **`commitIntakeToSessionAndServer`** — **`/justice/intake`** and **`/justice/chat`** → **`/justice/preview`** → **`/justice/plan`**; **`/justice/chat-ai`** signed-in **UUID** **create** stays in chat for inline funnel, with **`/justice/preview`** fallback when continuity guards fail. **Still unchanged on this slice:** **`rules.ts`**, readiness, preview draft **generation**, filing/evidence APIs, Supabase schema, **`POST /api/justice/intake-chat`** contract, auto-filing/submission automation (§1).

- **AI intake chat API (`POST /api/justice/intake-chat`):** **`src/app/api/justice/intake-chat/route.ts`** with **`buildJusticeIntakeAiPrompt.ts`** and **`parseIntakeChatAiResponse.ts`**. **Request:** `{ user_message, parts: BuildJusticeIntakeParts, conversation_history?: { role: "user" | "assistant"; content: string }[] }` — one user turn plus current partial parts and optional capped history. **Response:** `{ assistantMessage, parts }` — updated **`BuildJusticeIntakeParts`** (pre-commit; not full **`JusticeIntake`** until client runs **`buildJusticeIntakeFromParts`**). **Security:** same envelope as **`preview-draft`** — **`getUserOr401`**, **`rateLimit`**, **`OPENAI_API_KEY`** server-only, bounded body, JSON validation/clamping, OpenAI **`json_object`** response parsed before return. **No** Supabase / DB writes, **no** timeline writes, **no** case creation, **no** **`commitIntakeToSessionAndServer`** in the API. Shown for **fresh intake** and **hydrated Update in chat**. - **Chat AI intake — saved evidence count in Recap (Proof / evidence panel) (`/justice/chat-ai`):** **`src/app/justice/chat-ai/page.tsx`** only — **chat-first visibility** slice (with §2 **Chat AI intake — proof/evidence guidance**). When **Update in chat** is active (**`isUpdatingExistingCase`**) and the user is signed in with a **UUID** **`STORAGE_CASE_ID`**, page-local **`loadSavedEvidencePreview`** calls existing **`GET /api/justice/evidence?case_id={id}`** (same pattern as **`/justice/plan`** saved-evidence preview and **`/justice/cases`** progress fetch — **no** new route, **no** schema) and sets **`savedEvidenceCount`** plus **`recentEvidenceRows`** (up to 3 newest — §2 **Chat AI intake — recent saved proof preview in Recap (Proof / evidence panel)**). In **Recap → Proof / evidence**, shows **Saved evidence: {N} item(s).** when **N > 0** or **No saved evidence yet.** when **N === 0**; **no** count line on **fresh intake**, signed-out users, or non-UUID case ids (generic panel copy only). Refetches on **window** **focus** and tab **visibility** → **visible** and after in-chat proof note save (§2 **Chat AI intake — add proof note from Recap (Proof / evidence panel)**) so returning from **`/justice/evidence`** or saving in chat updates the count and recent preview. **Does not** create **`justice_case_evidence`** rows from chat except via §2 **Chat AI intake — add proof note from Recap (Proof / evidence panel)**; change **`POST /api/justice/intake-chat`**, **`commitIntakeToSessionAndServer`**, preview-readiness gating, **Current action tracking**, handling UI, **Organize evidence** link, or existing guidance copy. **No** migration, worker, **`justice_case_filings`**, timeline **type**, or external submission/contact/queue automation.
- **Chat AI intake — add proof note from Recap (Proof / evidence panel) (`/justice/chat-ai`):** **`src/app/justice/chat-ai/page.tsx`** only — **chat-first capture** slice (with §2 **Chat AI intake — proof/evidence guidance**, **Chat AI intake — saved evidence count in Recap (Proof / evidence panel)**, **Chat AI intake — recent saved proof preview in Recap (Proof / evidence panel)**, **Chat AI intake — edit recent proof note in Recap (Proof / evidence panel)**, **Chat AI intake — proof keyword nudge in Recap (Proof / evidence panel)**). When **Update in chat** is active (**`isUpdatingExistingCase`**) and the user is signed in with a **UUID** server-backed **`STORAGE_CASE_ID`** (**`canAddProofNoteInChat`** — same gate as **`loadSavedEvidencePreview`**: **`isLoaded`**, signed in, **`isUuid(caseId)`**), **Recap → Proof / evidence** shows a collapsed **`<details>`** **Add a proof note** mini-form: required **title** (max 500) and **evidence_type** select (**`JUSTICE_EVIDENCE_TYPES`** / **`JUSTICE_EVIDENCE_TYPE_LABELS`** from **`src/lib/justice/evidence.ts`**, default **`other`**); optional **evidence date** text input (max 200) and optional **description** textarea (max 8000). Submit **`POST /api/justice/evidence`** with **`case_id`**, **`title`**, **`evidence_type`**, and **`evidence_date`** / **`description`** only when trimmed non-empty — **no** new API, **no** schema; server appends **`evidence_added`** timeline via existing route. On success **`applyServerTimelineFromResponse`** (same pattern as **`/justice/evidence`** **`handleAdd`**), clears **title**, **evidence date**, and **description** ( **`evidence_type`** unchanged), shows **Proof note saved.**, refreshes **`loadSavedEvidencePreview`** (count + recent list — saved date/description appear in §2 **Chat AI intake — recent saved proof preview in Recap (Proof / evidence panel)** after refetch); on error, shows API **`error`** string; submit disabled while saving. **Metadata only** — honest copy (not file upload/storage); **no** **`source_url`** or **`storage_note`** in chat form; **no** filing, submission, external queue, or contact. **`/justice/evidence`** remains full list/edit/delete (**Organize evidence** link unchanged). On **Update in chat**, requires signed-in **UUID** **`STORAGE_CASE_ID`** (**`canAddProofNoteInChat`**). On **fresh intake**, stages locally via **`stagedProofNotes.ts`** (**`canStageProofNoteInChat`**) — §2 **Chat AI intake — staged proof notes on fresh intake (Proof / evidence panel)**; not signed-out. **No** auto-created evidence rows; **no** changes to **`POST /api/justice/intake-chat`** or **`buildJusticeIntakeAiPrompt.ts`** (§2 **Chat AI intake — proof keyword nudge in Recap (Proof / evidence panel)** is client-side in **`page.tsx`** only). **No** migration, worker, **`justice_case_filings`**, or external submission/contact/queue automation.
- **Chat AI intake — recent saved proof preview in Recap (Proof / evidence panel) (`/justice/chat-ai`):** **`src/app/justice/chat-ai/page.tsx`** only — **chat-first visibility** slice (with §2 **Chat AI intake — proof/evidence guidance**, **Chat AI intake — saved evidence count in Recap (Proof / evidence panel)**, **Chat AI intake — add proof note from Recap (Proof / evidence panel)**, **Chat AI intake — edit recent proof note in Recap (Proof / evidence panel)**, **Chat AI intake — delete recent proof note in Recap (Proof / evidence panel)**, **Chat AI intake — proof keyword nudge in Recap (Proof / evidence panel)**). Reuses the same **`loadSavedEvidencePreview`** **`GET /api/justice/evidence?case_id={id}`** response ( **`created_at` desc** ) — **no** second fetch. When **Update in chat** is active, signed in, **UUID** **`STORAGE_CASE_ID`**, and **`savedEvidenceCount > 0`** (**`showRecentEvidencePreview`**), **Recap → Proof / evidence** shows collapsed **`<details>`** **Recent proof notes** (up to **3** rows from **`recentEvidenceRows`**; summary **(3 of N)** when **N > 3**). Each row: **title**, **evidence_type** label (**`JUSTICE_EVIDENCE_TYPE_LABELS`**), optional **evidence_date**, optional truncated **description** (~120 chars — **`CHAT_EVIDENCE_DESC_PREVIEW_MAX`**); per-row **Edit** → inline form (§2 **Chat AI intake — edit recent proof note in Recap (Proof / evidence panel)**) and **Delete** (§2 **Chat AI intake — delete recent proof note in Recap (Proof / evidence panel)**); values saved/edited/deleted in chat appear after **`loadSavedEvidencePreview`** refetch; **no** **`source_url`** or **`storage_note`** in chat. **`/justice/evidence`** remains full list/edit/delete for all rows and optional links (**Organize evidence** unchanged). - **Chat AI intake — edit recent proof note in Recap (Proof / evidence panel) (`/justice/chat-ai`):** **`src/app/justice/chat-ai/page.tsx`** only — **chat-first limited edit** slice (with §2 **Chat AI intake — recent saved proof preview in Recap (Proof / evidence panel)**, **Chat AI intake — add proof note from Recap (Proof / evidence panel)**). In **Recent proof notes**, each displayed row (max **3**) has **Edit**; one inline form at a time with **title**, **evidence_type**, optional **evidence date** (max 200), optional **description** (max 8000), **Save** / **Cancel** — hydrated from full **`recentEvidenceRows`** row (not truncated preview text). **`PATCH /api/justice/evidence/[id]`** (existing route — **no** new API, **no** schema) with **`title`**, **`evidence_type`**, **`evidence_date`** (trimmed string or **`null`** to clear), **`description`** (trimmed string or **`null`** to clear) only — **no** **`source_url`** or **`storage_note`**. - **Chat AI intake — delete recent proof note in Recap (Proof / evidence panel) (`/justice/chat-ai`):** **`src/app/justice/chat-ai/page.tsx`** only — **chat-first limited delete** slice (with §2 **Chat AI intake — recent saved proof preview in Recap (Proof / evidence panel)**, **Chat AI intake — edit recent proof note in Recap (Proof / evidence panel)**). After a **successful** **`handleSend`** → **`POST /api/justice/intake-chat`** round trip, inspects the **latest user message** only (local regex in **`page.tsx`** — **no** API/schema changes; **`buildJusticeIntakeAiPrompt.ts`** unchanged). **Strong terms** (e.g. screenshot, receipt, invoice, tracking, confirmation, transcript, call note, chat log, account page); **negative guard** skips phrases like “no proof/evidence/screenshot”; **does not** match weak terms alone (proof, evidence, file, upload, email). When **`canAddProofNoteInChat`** and not yet offered this page session, shows a dismissible amber banner above **Add a proof note** guiding user to save a metadata proof note (**not** a file upload); **prefills** **Add a proof note** locally from the triggering user message (**empty fields only** — never overwrites an existing draft): **title** from trimmed/collapsed message capped ~**120** chars (word-safe ellipsis when truncated); **description** = full collapsed message only when longer than the title cap; **does not** infer **`evidence_type`** or **`evidence_date`**; opens the **Add a proof note** **`<details>`** for review; user must still click **Save proof note**. **Got it** dismisses the banner; banner hides after successful proof note save; **at most once** per page session. **Does not** auto-create **`justice_case_evidence`** rows. **Not** on fresh intake before first server commit. **LLM/system-prompt** proof nudges remain **future** work. **No** API/schema/intake-chat/prompt changes on this slice. **No** migration, worker, **`justice_case_filings`**, or external submission/contact/queue automation.
- **Chat AI intake — staged proof notes on fresh intake (Proof / evidence panel) (`/justice/chat-ai`):** **`src/app/justice/chat-ai/page.tsx`** + **`src/lib/justice/stagedProofNotes.ts`** — **client-side staging** slice (with §2 **Chat AI intake — add proof note from Recap (Proof / evidence panel)**). On **fresh intake** (**`!isUpdatingExistingCase`**, signed in — **`canStageProofNoteInChat`**), **Recap → Proof / evidence** **Add a proof note** **stages** metadata locally in **`sessionStorage`** key **`justice_staged_proof_notes_v1`** (**`readStagedProofNotes`** / **`appendStagedProofNote`** / **`removeStagedProofNotesByClientIds`**) — **title**, **`evidence_type`**, optional **`evidence_date`**, optional **`description`** only; **no** **`POST /api/justice/evidence`** until flush; honest copy (**Staged on this device until you save your case in chat**); read-only **pending** staged count/list whenever signed in and staged rows exist (**`showStagedProofNotes`** — not only during **`canStageProofNoteInChat`**); mount always hydrates **`stagedProofNotes`** from **`readStagedProofNotes()`** even when loading **Update in chat**; honest copy (**pending upload — Continue to save to your case** on loaded case vs **on this device until you save your case in chat** on fresh intake); **no** staged edit/delete in this slice. Shown whenever the post-draft callout is visible (same gate as proof-readiness and **Update in chat** lines — **not** a separate gate). **Does not** change **`showPostDraftReviewCallout`** gating, **`evidenceReady`**, **`readyToEscalate`**, **`recommendationText`**, **`pickPreparedNextAction`**, packet CTAs, handling/approval UI, readiness fetch, evidence/proof card logic, preview **Continue** behavior, timeline writes, APIs, schema, helpers, hub, cases, **`/justice/chat-ai`**, or **`/justice/preview`** implementation beyond the in-app link target. **Does not** claim filing, submission, contact, queueing, upload, storage, or automatic action by Surrenderless. **No** migration, worker, **`justice_case_filings`**, or external submission/contact/queue automation.
- **Plan — post-draft next-step explainer and readiness bridge (`/justice/plan`):** **`src/app/justice/plan/page.tsx`** only — **UI/copy** slice (with §2 **Plan — prepared next action after draft review (`/justice/plan`)**, §2 **Plan — proof readiness continuity after preview review (`/justice/plan`)**, §2 **Plan — post-draft chat continuity prompt after preview review (`/justice/plan`)**, §2 **Plan — post-draft re-preview continuity prompt after preview review (`/justice/plan`)**, §2 **Plan — post-draft approved step label alignment (`/justice/plan`)**, §2 **Packet — prepared review explainer and readiness bridge (`/justice/packet`)**, §2 **Packet — post-approval approved-step explainer and emerald card copy refresh (`/justice/packet`)**, §2 **Plan — Case readiness checklist proof CTA (`/justice/plan`)**, §2 **Plan — Case readiness checklist basics CTA (`/justice/plan`)**, §2 **Plan — Case readiness checklist draft-review CTA (`/justice/plan`)**, §2 **Plan — Case readiness checklist prepared packet reviewed row (`/justice/plan`)**). - **Chat AI intake — hydrate & update commit:** **`/justice/chat-ai`** is the in-app **Update in chat** path for an **active local case** (e.g. from **`/justice/plan`**, **Saved cases**, or hub — §2 **Saved cases — Needs more info chat routing CTA (`/justice/cases`)**, §2 **Justice hub — Needs more info chat routing CTA on Current case (`/justice`)**). **Hydration:** one-time mount read via **`readValidLocalJusticeIntake()`** → **`justiceIntakeToBuildJusticeIntakeParts`** in **`buildJusticeIntake.ts`** (shared with scripted/structured alignment); baseline **`parts`** snapshot for session change summary — §2 **Chat AI intake — session change summary (Update in chat)**. **Active case** orientation banner when hydrated — §2 **Chat AI intake — active case context banner (Update in chat)**; compact readiness checklist on **Update in chat** — §2 **Chat AI intake — active case compact readiness checklist (Update in chat) (`/justice/chat-ai`)**, §2 **Chat AI intake — active case prepared packet reviewed checklist row (Update in chat) (`/justice/chat-ai`)**; funnel-aware footer work links on **Active case** banner — §2 **Chat AI intake — active case banner work-link funnel routing (Update in chat) (`/justice/chat-ai`)**; same funnel-aware footer work links on **Recap → Current action tracking** when **`approvedNextAction`** exists — §2 **Chat AI intake — Recap current-action work-link funnel routing (Update in chat) (`/justice/chat-ai`)**; read-only approved next-step label/status on **Active case** banner when **`approvedNextAction`** exists — §2 **Chat AI intake — approved next-step label/status on Active case banner (Update in chat) (`/justice/chat-ai`)**. **Commit:** **`commitIntakeToSessionAndServer`** **`mode: "update"`** preserves **`STORAGE_CASE_ID`**, does **not** call **`newCaseId()`**, does **not** **`clearTimelineForNewCase`**, does **not** append **`case_started`**, does **not** clear FTC/mock keys, does **not** fire **`intake_completed`**, does **not** **`POST /api/justice/cases`**; writes **`STORAGE_INTAKE`**; when signed in and case id is a **UUID**, **`PATCH /api/justice/cases/[id]`** with `{ intake, timeline }` (same pattern as merchant save). **Create** **`mode`** (default) unchanged for new intake and for **`/justice/intake`** / **`/justice/chat`**. **`commitIntakeToSessionAndServer`** returns **`CommitIntakeResult`** **`{ caseId, serverPersisted }`** — **create** sets **`serverPersisted`** when signed-in **`POST /api/justice/cases`** succeeds with **`id`**; **update** sets **`serverPersisted`** when **`PATCH`** succeeds (callers may ignore; §2 **Chat AI intake — staged proof notes on fresh intake (Proof / evidence panel)** uses it before flushing staged proof). **No** new timeline event type for “intake updated” on this slice. **Limitations:** **`/justice/intake`** submit still uses **create** only (editing loaded session can still spawn a duplicate case — pre-existing); signed-out or non-UUID session ids get local intake update only (no server PATCH); **no** filing/submission automation.

- **AI chat intake — API error-copy polish (`/justice/chat-ai`):** **`src/app/justice/chat-ai/page.tsx`** only — page-local **`formatIntakeChatApiError(status, serverError)`** in **`handleSend`**: for **`!res.ok`** responses, replaces raw server **`error`** strings (e.g. **`Unauthorized`**, **`Invalid model JSON`**, **`OPENAI_API_KEY not configured`**) with clearer user-facing retry guidance — **401** (session expired, sign in and resend), **429** (wait and retry), **502** (usable AI reply), **500** (including missing-key vs generic server error), **400**, **413** / too-large body, and a generic fallback. **Success path**, **input** clearing on success, **retry** after failure (input/messages/**`parts`** preserved), **duplicate-send** guard, **Recap**, and **Continue** → **`/justice/preview`** unchanged. - **AI intake — `purchase_or_signup` extraction (`buildJusticeIntakeAiPrompt.ts`):** **Issue found:** on **`/justice/chat-ai`**, a user said a **“phone case”** never arrived; the assistant repeated “phone case” in **`assistantMessage`** but returned **`parts.purchase_or_signup`** empty, so the recap **Product / service** line stayed blank and the pre-preview basics gate blocked. **Fix (prompt-only):** **`src/lib/justice/buildJusticeIntakeAiPrompt.ts`** now explicitly instructs the model to populate **`purchase_or_signup`** whenever the product, service, order item, subscription, account, charge target, or thing purchased/charged is **clearly stated** (with examples such as phone case, Prime, checking account, internet plan) — without inventing when unstated. **No** change to **`parseIntakeChatAiResponse.ts`**, **`/justice/chat-ai`** page, API route behavior, commit helper, preview/plan, or scripted chat. **Smoke-tested:** **`/justice/chat-ai`** now maps **“phone case”** into **Product / service** and a complete intake reaches **`/justice/preview`**.

On **`window` `focus`** and on **`document` `visibilitychange`** when **`visibilityState === "visible"`**, re-runs **`loadCases`**, replaces in-memory **`cases`** and **`has_more`** on success, and preserves existing load-error behavior (**`Could not load cases.`** + empty list on failure). Refetch uses **`offset=0`** and **`limit = Math.max(casesLengthRef.current, CASES_PAGE_LIMIT)`** so a user who used **Load more** does **not** shrink back to only the first page after refocus (still subject to API **`MAX_LIST_LIMIT`** cap). **`refreshSessionCaseIdFromStorage`** on the same events keeps **Current case in this browser** aligned. **Purpose:** when the user returns to an open **Saved cases** tab after **Mark acknowledged** on **`/justice/plan`** or **`/justice/chat-ai`**, **Needs attention**, **All cases** handling blocks (**`CaseApprovedNextActionTracking`**), **display-only** queue status, and handled/open triage notes (§2 **Saved cases — handled/open handling triage note on All cases cards**) rebucket from fresh **`client_state`** without a full page reload. **Cases-local Mark acknowledged** still updates **`cases`** immediately via **`applyAcknowledgedHandlingToCaseRow`** — refocus refetch is additive, not required for on-page ack. **Does not** change **Needs attention** inclusion (**`isHandlingAwaitingTriageApprovedNextAction`**), **Mark acknowledged** on active handling **Needs attention** cards, **Open case**, **search** / **filter** / **sort**, **Load more** append semantics, archive/labels, workbench **Awaiting** / nested handled / **Acknowledged** membership, APIs, schema, persistence, or external-action behavior. **No** migration, worker, **`justice_case_filings`**, timeline **type**, or external submission/contact/queue automation; Surrenderless has **not** filed, submitted, sent, **queued externally**, or contacted anyone.

Copy: **Next action recorded as handled**; **in-app tracking only** — Surrenderless has **not** filed, submitted, sent, or contacted anyone. **`resolveApprovedNextAction`** on plan, packet, and chat **does not downgrade** **`completed`** → **`started`** → **`approved`**. **`/justice/packet`** hydrates and shows handled/completed state in the approval area (record handled from plan or chat). When **`approved_next_action`** exists in **Recap** **Current action tracking** and **`handling_requested_at`** is **missing** (and **`status !== "completed"`**), shows **Request Surrenderless handling** with the same **optional short note** as plan; click sets **`approved_next_action.handling_requested_at`** (ISO) and optional **`handling_request_note`** while **preserving** **`status`**, **`href`**, **`label`**, timestamps, **`outcome_note`**, and **`follow_up_*`**.
